As far as the apartments, they‚Äôre on the small side. Measure your furniture if you‚Äôre getting a 1br. Honestly the 2brs seem to be a better deal as they‚Äôre only a little more and you get a second bathroom. Having said that, the amenities are very nice. If you‚Äôre coming from a place where you shared laundry, you‚Äôll never want to go back. The gym and pools are well maintained, and the landscapers do a great job keeping the place looking good.

There are a few negatives.
-The apartments seem a little on the pricey side for the size, but that‚Äôs subjective. I don‚Äôt feel like I‚Äôm overpaying compared to the hovel I lived in in Carlsbad, and I‚Äôm not aware of many complexes in SD at this price point that are this well run.
-The speed bumps are the bane of my existence. I like that people aren‚Äôt blasting through the parking lot, but my shocks have taken a beating.

<gmap_id>0x809b71f99b339d71:0x40b9559c3e363e09< /gmap_id><review>The food was good but many other things were wrong. Health concerns.

It pains me to give a bad review but I hope it helps the business do better next time.
First of all I work in food service, I was out of work for a long time due to COVID-19 and it was hard finding a new job I lost a lot of income this year so my review has no political background.
I was excited to see this type of food and was eager to try it, I saw the tables outside with some deliciously looking plates so I had to try it.

My wife ordered and I went in to pick up the order, as I waited for the order I noticed how the person on the line plating the food was not wearing gloves, according to the California food code contact with ready to eat food (won't have any further preparation to be eaten) should be done with disposable gloves. Its the kind of stuff health inspectors fine during inspections.
The cashier who was handling cash from the tip jar jumped in to help plating the orders not wearing gloves, more importantly not washing his hands before touching the food. One of the cooks was opening some bags of condiments with his teeth.
None in the kitchen was wearing a face mask except the cashier.
I know the mask is uncomfortable in a hot kitchen by own experience, but its a reality we have to face for a few more months.
A close friend lost his father to COVID, a high-school classmate also died recently to the virus.

I didn't enjoy my food wondering if this was safe to eat or not.<//review><name>Joaquin Davalos<//name>< pics>

<name>Alex Reed<//name>< Review>
I discovered Meze at an event at the North Colombia School House before Meze opened down town. I was impressed with the quality and freshness of the food, as well as the authenticity and flavor of my  Falafel Plate. Service was friendly and prompt.
When Meze opened I was one of the first customers and enjoyed my beef and lamb gyro, with hot sauce. No complaints, although I thought the price tag of around $14 for a gyro seemed high, despite that the ingredients are claimed to be organic. I have tried and love the Vegan Bowl as well ( even though Im far from Vegan ).
The only complaint that I have is the tables are often dirty with food from the last person who sat there. I asked for the table to be cleaned once and the woman behind the counter begrudgingly came out and wiped the table, knocking food bits on to the floor, and my lap to my dismay. The table still had a layer of black grime that I had to wipe off with a paper napkin so that I could feel good about eating off the table. The bathroom trash is often over flowing, and there has been empty soap dispenser in the bathroom.
Overall, the food is very good, the front end could be more friendly , but I like this place and would and do continue to frequent this establishment. Glad you are here in our community. Give thanks!!</Review>

115599545290522223554</userid>

Vilina Hutter< /Name>
< Date>
1551983601987</Date>
<rating>4< /rating>< review>
Really new and different food for Grass Valley, MeZe offers Israeli/middle eastern food in a casual environment.   Typical menu items are in the range of $15 .  You can order pitas sandwiches or plates, which feature meat or falafel, for example,  with small servings of salads and dressings.   I've had both a sandwich and a falafel plate.  I enjoyed both, but the falafel was just a touch over crisp and dry.  Still good if dipped in sauce!
Food is ordered at the register, and your name is called when it's ready.  Someone needs to explain to me why a tip is suggested by the cash register software.  Since when do cashiers get tips?  Also, the cashier is responsible for the phone, which means divided attention.   Have someone else do the take out orders!
Seating is quite limited in this small eatery...less than 6 small tables and a counter.  Nowhere is comfort a consideration...the chairs are functional but do not encourage lingering!
The service can be kind of strange.  Pita sandwich halfs are served on a rack, oddly lodged into coffee filters.  That's just wierd, and not actually very effective for drippy hand held food like this.  Hopefully they will plow some of their profits into a better service solution!
Overall, this is  worthwhile place.  The prime mission of a restaurant is to serve good food, and MeZe does that.  It's fresh, made from scratch, unusual flavors, and plenty of vegetarian options.  The price is reasonable.  It's not  a comfy hang out dinner place, for sure, but for a quick tasty and healthy dinner, it is great.  And I bet the peripheral details will improve as they are in business longer.<//review>

<rate>4</rate>< Text>
What I've tried on my first visit: Grasshopper, salted caramel, and banana dulce de leche macaron ice cream sandwiches.  I've also tried the peanut butter brownie, blue velvet cake, and red velvet cupcake.  Out of the three macaron ice cream sandwiches I've tried is the banana dulce de leche.  The grasshopper is mint ice cream and the sandwich is dipped in dark chocolate; the salted caramel is self-descriptive; the banana dulce de leche has a nice flavor of banana and is nicely combined with caramel -- the sandwiches are not so sweet.  The blue velvet cake is just okay, it has blueberries but I love their red velvet cupcake! It taste better than the blue velvet IMHO.  The brownie is just a regular brownie.  Next time if I'm around the area, I will try their milk shake and customize my own ice cream sandwich with their cookies.< /Text>

Situated in Oakland, CA the Coral Reef Inn and Suites is just a couple of hundred feet from the water edge with a view across to San Francisco city. We stayed in a self contained unit with a separate kitchen, dining area and lounge area with a seperate bathroom and two bedroom, plenty of storage space and a private covered balcony area with a small waterway in front with bird life and even a raccoon. < Text>
The hotel furniture is a little runned down but I can look past it.  It's in a great location, it feels safe, a shopping mall across the street and next to the shore where you can run or walk and enjoy the view.  The hotel does not have a gym on the property but they give you a pass to use Rise Bodyworks which is a full gym.  I love this!!!  The gym is 2 blocks away, it's a 10 minute walk or 3 minute drive, but parking sucks.  Any pots and pans you may need you get from a room around from the lobby.  The breakfast in my opinion is not that great.  All sugar and no protein.   It's composed of raisin bran cereal, donuts, danishes, toast and jelly.  Of course coffee, tea and orange juice is available.   I prefer just to go to Safeway or Trader Joe's across the street and get a better breakfast.   The staff is friendly, free parking and plenty of it, I see myself staying here again!</Text>

< Text>
Think "Old Motel". The rooms have an off odor and are kinda clean just don't look too close. Carpets are stained. No signs of bedbugs in the bed frames/mattress. We stayed twice at the beginning and end of a trip since we were flying out of OAK. Uber cost between $11 to $13 to go from OAK and Coral Reef Inn.  Our rooms had a mini frig. and kitchenette but no dishes or pans, you have to ask the desk to find this stuff in a side room. The offer free breakfast which is coffee/OJ with packaged danishes, cold cereal, yogurt and donuts. For us it's a lot of sugary carbs that got old quick but to each their own. A few times we asked the front desk for information about things to do in the area. They we quite helpful and provided good times to account for traffic. Directly across the street is a nice/new strip plaza. The plaza has a gas station, drugstore, Trader Joe's (open 9-9) and a Safeway grocery open 24 hours. It's an OK place for our needs, if ever flying into OAK again I would probably look around some more.< /Text>

<text>Fantastic. I would live here. Apartments converted to a hotel. Great location across the street from shopping, including a grocery store, which makes cooking and eating in super convenient. Stove, fridge, microwave, cookware provided (ask for it at the front desk). Sushi restaurant down the street is excellent also.

For convenient entertainment, there is a bowling alley next door, with a bar, and food, music and other amenities. It's noisy/lively, if your into that, very it just want something to do, or somewhere to go. No driving necessary!

Only thing missing is a closer gym (my kind of entertainment), but there is a 24 Hour Fitness and an Anytime Fitness within driving distance.
They had passes to a local gym (if you inquire about gym access), but that gym had long been closed down, so double check before going, if they do have passes available.
Hopefully, they will find another gym to partner with.

Room could be a bit cleaner.

At the time the phone system was out. Had been down for many months. They said they will be fixing it, but given how long it's been it, I'm not so sure. So if this is important for you, do inquire geometry booking.
Fortunately cell phones make this less necessary.  Note you cannot contact the front desk or get a wake up call.
Not a big deal, but they should have put a note in the room, it at least stated so at check in, so I did not waste time/effort trying to contact them from my room.

Overall enjoyed my stay. The apartment-like feel was comfortable and a refreshing change from chain hotels. Walkability to stores (including grocery) was also welcomed.

<rating>4<//rating><Review>As a budget accommodation, I give Coral Reef Inn 4 stars because one would be hard pressed to find similarly clean, safe accommodations in this area for about $99 - 120 (off season) per night.  Please read the whole review for a full understanding of the accommodation.
Having said that, Coral Reef is very worn and shows the upgrades over the decades very clearly.  I find this type of archeological survey interesting - the owners would do well to bring it back to its mid-century splendor and get rid of the additions from the 70s on.
The rooms are huge.  If you have children, this could be a great budget place to stay because the units are old apartments with full living room, bedroom, kitchen, lots of closets and big bathroom.
Our bed was very troubling though.  It was dented and worn and not very comfortable.  This could be a deal breaker for many - even if they're trying to go cheap.
If you have mobility issues, make sure to get a ground floor room.  Entrances to the units go directly outside.  There are no elevators to the 2nd floor and the stairs are open concrete, outside the building.  The grounds are large and you may have to take a short hike to your room some people may have trouble with.
But we HAD to go cheap a few nights of our trip, and so - this suited.  It was safe, clean in spite of the shabbiness, and adjacent to tons of shopping and restaurants in Alameda.</Review>< userid>

< text>
My husband and I spent 6 days here in early August in a Lagood Suite.  The carpet in the room was dirty, turning my white socks black in no time.  The furniture was dated and badly scratched.  The drapes in the bedroom were worn out and starting to shred at the time and were full of holes.  The surface of the stove was covered in grease.  The railing on the balcony was filthy and could not be touched without getting you dirty.    The towels were far from luxurious.  They were soaking wet when you finished drying off.  The breakfast they offered consisted of stale cereal, some fresh and some stale bread, weak coffee.  They also offered donuts and yogurt which were good, so we stuck to them.  The lobby, grounds and pool are kept up so you think the place is up to date, but it drastically needs remodeling.  We stayed here 6 years ago and it was much better.  We will not be coming back.  The only reason we stayed this time was because all of the local hotels were full and we could not find another room.  The only good thing about the place was the bed was comfortable, but even that had a flaw (the bottom fitted sheet did not fit so they split the  corner to make it fit.  Tacky.</text>

Breakfast wasn't that bad and you could sit down in the lobby and eat or take everything with you to your room, where there was a dining table anyway.

The environment is ok. There are many shops and fast food restaurants across from the motel. The beach is less than 100 meters away. And getting to San Francisco by car was no problem.
The motel is cheap, especially for the location, it's a huge plus! From the price-performance ratio it was fine. I would book it again.
